<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschaamd.html>beschaamd</a> (8267)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beschaemt</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>Past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschamen.html>beschamen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschaamd.html>beschaamd</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschaamd.html>beschaamder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">beschaamdst</b>)

<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:juridisch.html>juridisch</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:besluit.html>besluit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wettelijk.html>wettelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:juridisch.html>juridisch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regelt.html>regelt</a>
